\hypertarget{interfaceMathLinSpace__mod_1_1getLinSpace}{}\doxysection{Math\+Lin\+Space\+\_\+mod\+::get\+Lin\+Space Interface Reference}
\label{interfaceMathLinSpace__mod_1_1getLinSpace}\index{MathLinSpace\_mod::getLinSpace@{MathLinSpace\_mod::getLinSpace}}


Return the {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} output argument with {\ttfamily size(\+Lin\+Space)} elements of evenly-\/spaced values over the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}x1, x2\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily x1 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x2}, or {\ttfamily \mbox{[}x2, x1\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily x2 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x1}.  




\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Return the {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} output argument with {\ttfamily size(\+Lin\+Space)} elements of evenly-\/spaced values over the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}x1, x2\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily x1 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x2}, or {\ttfamily \mbox{[}x2, x1\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily x2 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x1}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Lin\+Space} & \+: The output contiguous array of type either {\ttfamily real} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aaf5c6c840ed0befe5a37da626c35716f}{RK32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a855643f887b4c787e6542e9e7849680f}{RK64}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aeef7c44b90b75aeeebdef1da504886cb}{RK128}} or {\ttfamily complex} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ac8b456bd9511bc9a52b4a03bda4b72df}{CK32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aa6ea61256fca0b20db0ec2b90755b9f3}{CK64}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ad3873e1ecc5eb3cf3651f72630cae087}{CK128}} containing the evenly spaced numbers. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em x1} & \+: The input scalar of the same type and kind as {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} representing the starting value of the sequence. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em x2} & \+: The input scalar of the same type and kind as {\ttfamily x1} representing the ending value of the sequence. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em fopen} & \+: The input scalar of type {\ttfamily logical} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a68ac316f10b57be996670bc7c0abed9d}{LK}}. If {\ttfamily .true.}, the {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} will be {\bfseries{f}}irst-\/open, meaning that {\ttfamily x1} will NOT be in the output {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} sequence ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily .false.}). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em lopen} & \+: The input scalar of type {\ttfamily logical} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a68ac316f10b57be996670bc7c0abed9d}{LK}}. If {\ttfamily .true.}, the {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} will be {\bfseries{l}}ast-\/open, meaning that {\ttfamily x2} will NOT be in the output {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} sequence ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily .false.}).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This procedure is {\ttfamily pure}.

Setting both {\ttfamily fopen = .true.} and {\ttfamily lopen = .true.} will lead to an output {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} whose points are centers of the {\ttfamily count + 1} equally-\/sized bins in the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}x1,x2\mbox{]}}.

If {\ttfamily Lin\+Space} has a size of {\ttfamily 1} while {\ttfamily fopen = .false.} and {\ttfamily lopen = .false.}, then {\ttfamily Lin\+Space = \mbox{[}x1\mbox{]}} on return.
\end{DoxyRemark}
